Thanks, Angela, and good morning, everyone. I wanted to kick off by acknowledging that last week we closed our merger transaction with Liberty TripAdvisor Holdings, in which we effectively purchased all of our shares held by LTRIP and no longer have a controlling shareholder. Compared to last year, adjusted EBITDA benefited from lower personnel costs, which offset increases in cost of sales and marketing. Turning now to consolidated expenses for the quarter.
